<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoffel.html>schoffel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shovel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skuflō</i>.
</p>

***schokken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schokken.html>schokken</a> (16780)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, cognate with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shock</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schokken.html>schokken</a></strong>
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schokken.html>schokken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To shake, shiver
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vanwege.html>Vanwege</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> ijsvorming <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spoor.html>spoor</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schokte.html>schokte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> passagierstrein <a href = vnd.unilang:hevig.html>hevig</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Because of the <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a> and the formation of ice on the <a href = vnd.unilang:tracks.html>tracks</a>, the passenger train <b><a href = vnd.unilang:shook.html>shook</a></b> vehemently.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To (administer a) shock physically</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To shock, disturb, startle

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schol.html>schol</a> (35645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schil.html>schil</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schel.html>schel</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Scholle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">floe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schol.html>schol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schollen.html>schollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scholletje.html>scholletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>floating plate (e.g. ice floe or tectonic plate)
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ice floe</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ijsschol</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsschots.html>ijsschots</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schots.html>schots</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sod.html>sod</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">clod</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">turf</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">lump of earth, sometimes with vegetation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:schol.html>schol</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schône</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum">schônen</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to make/become beautiful, to decorate</li>
<li>to improve, to make/become better</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">Skáney</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schonen.html>schonen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Scania</span> (a region)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

***schooien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schooien.html>schooien</a> (59295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schooien.html>schooien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to travel around in freedom without a plan or profession, to wander</li>
<li>to beg, implore, beseech</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bedelen.html>bedelen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">school</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">school</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ziek.html>ziek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoonbroer.html>schoonbroer</a> (21495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoon.html>schoon</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">beau-frere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoonbroer.html>schoonbroer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoonbroers.html>schoonbroers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoonbroer.html>schoonbroertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brother-in-law</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoonbroer.html>schoonbroer</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly used in Belgium and the southern Dutch provinces Limburg and North Brabant. In the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of the Netherlands, the more common word for “brother-in-law” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zwager.html>zwager</a></i>, but <i><a href = vnd.unilang:schoonbroer.html>schoonbroer</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> naturally understood from association.
</p>

</p>

***schoorsteen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoorsteen.html>schoorsteen</a> (8781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoorsteen.html>schoorsteen</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoren.html>schoren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to support</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steen.html>steen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally meaning a fireplace supporting a smoke channel, like the word <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">chimney</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoorsteen.html>schoorsteen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoorstenen.html>schoorstenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoorsteen.html>schoorsteentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">chimney</span> (vertical tube or hollow column; a <span class="Latn" lang="en">flue</span>).</li>
<li>The smokestack of a steamboat or steam locomotive.</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:schoorsteen.html>schoorsteen</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li>rookkanaal <a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> stookplaats
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dertig.html>dertig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoge.html>hoge</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schoorsteen.html>schoorsteen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:levensgevaarlijk.html>levensgevaarlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgebroken.html>afgebroken</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schieten.html>schote</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schuete</i>, the same as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheut.html>scheut</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoot.html>schoot</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skautaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoot.html>schoot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoten.html>schoten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schootje.html>schootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lap, upper <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:madonna.html>Madonna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kindje.html>kindje</a> Jezus <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoot.html>schoot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:zetel.html>zetel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijsheid.html>Wijsheid</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:genoemd.html>genoemd</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:madonna.html>Madonna</a> with <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a> Jesus on her lap <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called the "seat of Wisdom".</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Various corresponding parts of certain vestments, animals and <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a></li>
<li>A shoot, certain ropes or chains used in sailing</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">lap</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoothond.html>schoothond</a> (59285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoot.html>schoot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schoßhund</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoothond.html>schoothond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoothond.html>schoothonden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoothondje.html>schoothondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">lapdog</span>, a canine pet which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> small and/or frequently <span class="Latn" lang="en">cuddled</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A human, (nearly) willless '<span class="Latn" lang="en">pet</span>' or <span class="Latn" lang="en">flunky</span>.</li></ol>

</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoppen.html>schoppen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoppen.html>schoppens</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoppen.html>schoppen</a></strong></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoppen.html>schoppentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:spades.html>spades</a></li>
<li>a playing card of the <a href = vnd.unilang:spades.html>spades</a> suit</li></ol>

***schorpioen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schorpioen.html>schorpioen</a> (11126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scorpioen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">scorpion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scorpiō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σκορπίος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skorpíos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schorpioen.html>schorpioen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schorpioenen.html>schorpioenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schorpioen.html>schorpioentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A scorpion, an arachnid with a venomous sting of the order Scorpiones.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:scorpio.html>scorpio</a>, an ancient single-arm catapult.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scorpio.html>scorpio</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A vicious, dangerous person; tormentor.</li>
<li>Vernacular names for other species:
<ol><li>the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_mole_cricket" class="extiw" title="w:European mole cricket">European mole cricket</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gryllotalpa_gryllotalpa" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gryllotalpa gryllotalpa"><i>Gryllotalpa gryllotalpa</i></a></span></li>
<li>a certain weed; shortened from the derived term schorpioenkruid</li></ol></li>
<li>A scourge, a flail with sharp <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> used for flogging.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li>(other animal species) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schorpioenkreeft</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schorpioenspin</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schorpioenvis</span> (obsolete spelling schorpioenvisch), <span class="Latn" lang="nl">stekelschorpioenvis</span> (obsolete spelling stekelschorpioenvisch), <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schorpioenvlieg</span></li>
<li>(plant species) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schorpioenkroonkruid</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, schorpioenkruid <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">schorpioenwortel</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schors.html>schors</a> (21494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scorce</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">escorce</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">écorce</i>), itself from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scorcia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scortea</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>Bark, (tree) surface tissue</li>
<li>Any equivalent rind on other plants</li>
<li>A similar exterior tissue or layer, peel or crust, e.g. on an organ</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One's or something's appearance; a cover</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> another rough and/or protective exterior or ice</li></ol>

***schorsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schorsen.html>schorsen</a> (14903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schorsen.html>schorsen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">escorcier</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*excurtiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schorsen.html>schorsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suspend, delay (an event, proceding) by inserting a pause
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorzitter.html>voorzitter</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:schorst.html>schorst</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zitting.html>zitting</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The chairman <b>suspends</b> the session.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opschorten.html>opschorten</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suspend, temporarily depose / remove from office or from membership or enrolment in an organisation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdachten.html>verdachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> ambtshalve <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geschorst.html>geschorst</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The suspects are <b>suspended</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>ex</a> officio.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schort.html>schort</a> (11786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schorte</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schort.html>schort</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schorten.html>schorten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schortje.html>schortje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>apron (clothing)</li></ol>

***schot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schot.html>schot</a> (1877)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schot.html>schot</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skutą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skot</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">skoz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schot.html>schot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoten.html>schoten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schotje.html>schotje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>shot, act of shooting</li>
<li>missile, projectile</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorschot.html>voorschot</a></span></li></ul>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schieten.html>schieten</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">scot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">partition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skut</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skot</i>. Further etymology unclear, but likely related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schut.html>schutten</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schott</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schot.html>schot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schotten.html>schotten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schotje.html>schotje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a divider that partitions a larger space into <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a> (traditionally wooden planks, but could be made of any materials)</li></ol>

***schotel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schotel.html>schotel</a> (7383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">scutella</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schüssel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***schouwen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schouwen.html>schouwen</a> (79730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schouwen.html>schouwen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">skouwon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skawwōną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kewh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schouwen.html>schouwen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to see, watch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to inspect formally, as with an honor guard</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to examine physically, as in forensics</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to see mentally</li></ol>

***schraal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schraal.html>schraal</a> (53292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dry; poor, scanty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, either from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skrēla-</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skrēha-</i>. Further origin uncertain.
</p><p>Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schriel</i> (regional), <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schrao</i> (dialectal), cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">skriel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schrāh</i> (dialectal), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">schrā</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poor, scanty, miserable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skrá</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dried skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and its descendants.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schraal.html>schraal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schraal.html>schraler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">schraalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poor, scanty</li></ol>

***schrapen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schrapen.html>schrapen</a> (16777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:schrapen.html>schrapen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scrape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skrapōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scrape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skreb-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*skrep-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to engrave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Forms doublets with Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schrappen.html>schrappen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strike through; to cancel; to scrap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schrabben</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scratch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schrabbelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scratch repeatedly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scrape</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scrap</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scrab</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schrapen.html>schrapen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to scrape</li>
<li>to rake</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:schrapen.html>schrapen</a></b>
</p>

***schreeuwen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:schreeuwen.html>schreeuwen</a> (2051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schrêwen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*skrēwon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skraiwōną</i>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schreien.html>schreien</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schreeuwen.html>schreeuwen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To yell; to bellow; to shout; to talk loudly.</li>
<li>To scream; to shriek.</li>
<li>Of a colour or design: to be extremely conspicuous.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:behang.html>behang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schreeuwt.html>schreeuwt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nogal.html>nogal</a>.</i>  |  This wallpaper <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rather loud.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gillen.html>gillen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krijsen.html>krijsen</a></span></li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schreeuw.html>schreeuw</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
